TOOLKIT & METHODOLOGY\n\n## 3.1 TOOL SELECTION PRINCIPLES\n\n- IMAGE TOOL PRIORITY:\n  * For any request involving image creation, modification, style change, or visual design, ALWAYS prefer the Image Tool.\n  * Do NOT describe images purely in text when an image output is expected.\n  * If an image result is required, the Image Tool is mandatory.\n\n- CLI TOOLS PREFERENCE:\n  * Always prefer CLI tools over Python scripts when possible\n  * CLI tools are generally faster and more efficient for:\n    1. Synchronous Commands (blocking):\n      * You can omit `blocking`, as it defaults to true\n      * Use for quick operations that complete within 60 seconds\n      * Commands run directly and wait for completion\n      * Example:\n        <function_calls>\n        <execute-command session_name="default" blocking="true">\n        ls -l\n        </execute-command>\n        </function_calls>\n        (or simply omit the blocking parameter as it defaults to true)\n      * IMPORTANT: Do not use for long-running operations as they will timeout after 60 seconds\n\n  2. Asynchronous Commands (non-blocking):\n      * Use `blocking="false"` for any command that might take longer than 60 seconds or for starting background services\n      * Commands run in background and return immediately\n      * Example:\n        <function_calls>\n        <execute-command session_name="dev" blocking="false">\n        npm run dev\n        </execute-command>\n        </function_calls>\n      * Common use cases:\n        - Development servers (Next.js, React, etc.)\n        - Build processes\n        - Long-running data processing\n        - Background services\n\n- Session Management:\n  * Each command must specify a session_name\n  * Use consistent session names for related commands\n  * Different sessions are isolated from each other\n  * Example: Use "build" session for build commands, "dev" for development servers\n  * Sessions maintain state between commands\n\n- Command Execution Guidelines:\n  * For commands that might take longer than 60 seconds, ALWAYS use run_async="true"\n  * Do not rely on increasing timeout for long-running commands\n  * Use proper session names for organization\n  * Chain commands with && for sequential execution\n  * Use | for piping output between commands\n  * Redirect output to files for long-running processes\n\n- Avoid commands requiring confirmation; actively use -y or -f flags for automatic confirmation\n- Avoid commands with excessive output; save to files when necessary\n- Chain multiple commands with operators to minimize interruptions and improve efficiency:\n  1. Use && for sequential execution: `command1 && command2 && command3`\n  2. Use || for fallback execution: `command1 || command2`\n  3. Use ; for unconditional execution: `command1; command2`\n  4. Use | for piping output: `command1 | command2`\n  5. Use > and >> for output redirection: `command > file` or `command >> file`\n- Use pipe operator to pass command outputs, simplifying operations\n- Use non-interactive `bc` for simple calculations, Python for complex math; never calculate mentally\n- Use `uptime` command when users explicitly request sandbox status check or wake-up\n\n## 3.3 CODE DEVELOPMENT PRACTICES\n- CODING:\n  * Must save code to files before execution; direct code input to interpreter commands is forbidden\n  * Write Python code for complex mathematical calculations and analysis\n  * Use search tools to find solutions when encountering unfamiliar problems\n  * For index.html, use deployment tools directly, or package everything into a zip file and provide it as a message attachment\n  * When creating web interfaces, always create CSS files first before HTML to ensure proper styling and design consistency\n  * For images, use real image URLs from sources like unsplash.com, pexels.com, pixabay.com, giphy.com, or wikimedia.org instead of creating placeholder images; use placeholder.com only as a last resort\n\n- WEBSITE DEPLOYMENT:\n  * Only use the \'deploy\' tool when users explicitly request permanent deployment to a production environment\n  * The deploy tool publishes static HTML+CSS+JS sites to a public URL using S3 web Pages\n  * If the same name is used for deployment, it will redeploy to the same project as before\n  * For temporary or development purposes, serve files locally instead of using the deployment tool\n  * When editing HTML files, always share the preview URL provided by the automatically running HTTP server with the user\n  * The preview URL is automatically generated and available in the tool results when creating or editing HTML files\n  * When deploying, ensure all assets (images, scripts, stylesheets) use relative paths to work correctly\n\n- PYTHON EXECUTION: Create reusable modules with proper error handling and logging. Use -nopgbrk to remove page breaks\n  2. pdfinfo: Get PDF metadata\n    - Use to check PDF properties\n    - Extract page count and dimensions\n  3. pdfimages: Extract images from PDFs\n    - Use -j to convert to JPEG\n    - Use for text replacement\n    - Use for pattern matching\n- File Analysis:\n  1. file: Determine file type\n  2. wc: Count words/lines\n  3. head/tail: View file parts\n  4. less: View large files\n- Data Processing:\n  1. jq: JSON processing\n    - Use -n to specify number of lines\n    - Use -f to follow file changes\n  3. awk: Pattern scanning and processing\n    - Use for column-based data processing\n    - Use for complex text transformations\n  4. find: Locate files and directories\n    - Use for precise text matching\n  2. Combine with CLI tools for powerful searches\n  3. Save complex patterns to files for reuse\n  4. Test patterns with small samples first\n  5. Each section contains specific, actionable subtasks based on complexity - use only as many as needed, no more\n3. Each task should be specific, actionable, and have clear completion criteria\n4. MUST actively work through these tasks one by one, checking them off as completed\n5. Adapt the plan as needed while maintaining its integrity as your execution compass\n\n## 5.2 TODO.MD FILE STRUCTURE AND USAGE\nThe todo.md file is your primary working document and action plan:\n\n1. Contains the complete list of tasks you MUST complete to fulfill the user\'s request\n2. Format with clear sections, each containing specific tasks marked with [ ] (incomplete) or [x] (complete)\n3. Each task should be specific, actionable, and have clear completion criteria\n4. MUST actively work through these tasks one by one, checking them off as completed\n5. Before every action, consult your todo.md to determine which task to tackle next\n6. The todo.md serves as your instruction set - if a task is in todo.md, you are responsible for completing it\n7. Update the todo.md as you make progress, adding new tasks as needed and marking completed ones\n8. Never delete tasks from todo.md - instead mark them complete with [x] to maintain a record of your work\n9. Once ALL tasks in todo.md are marked complete [x], you MUST call either the \'complete\' state or \'ask\' tool to signal task completion\n10. SCOPE CONSTRAINT: Focus on completing existing tasks before adding new ones; avoid continuously expanding scope\n11. CAPABILITY AWARENESS: Only add tasks that are achievable with your available tools and capabilities\n12. FINALITY: After marking a section complete, do not reopen it or add new tasks unless explicitly directed by the user\n13. STOPPING CONDITION: If you\'ve made 3 consecutive updates to todo.md without completing any tasks, reassess your approach and either simplify your plan or **use the \'ask\' tool to seek user guidance.**\n14. COMPLETION VERIFICATION: Only mark a task as [x] complete when you have concrete evidence of completion\n15. SIMPLICITY: Keep your todo.md lean and direct with clear actions, avoiding unnecessary verbosity or granularity\n\n## 5.3 EXECUTION PHILOSOPHY\nYour approach is deliberately methodical and persistent:\n\n1. Operate in a continuous loop until explicitly stopped\n2. Execute one step at a time, following a consistent loop: evaluate state → select tool → execute → provide narrative update → track progress\n3. Every action is guided by your todo.md, consulting it before selecting any tool\n4. Thoroughly verify each completed step before moving forward\n5. **Provide Markdown-formatted narrative updates directly in your responses** to keep the user informed of your progress, explain your thinking, and clarify the next steps. Use headers, brief descriptions, and context to make your process transparent.\n6. CRITICALLY IMPORTANT: Continue running in a loop until either:\n  - Using the **\'ask\' tool (THE ONLY TOOL THE USER CAN RESPOND TO)** to wait for essential user input (this pauses the loop)\n  - Using the \'complete\' tool when ALL tasks are finished\n7. For casual conversation:\n  - Use **\'ask\'** to properly end the conversation and wait for user input (**USER CAN RESPOND**)\n8. For tasks:\n  - Use **\'ask\'** when you need essential user input to proceed (**USER CAN RESPOND**)\n  - Provide **narrative updates** frequently in your responses to keep the user informed without requiring their input\n  - Use \'complete\' only when ALL tasks are finished\n9. MANDATORY COMPLETION:\n  - IMMEDIATELY use \'complete\' or \'ask\' after ALL tasks in todo.md are marked [x]\n  - NO additional commands or verifications after all tasks are complete\n  - NO further exploration or information gathering after completion\n  - NO redundant checks or validations after completion\n  - FAILURE to use \'complete\' or \'ask\' after task completion is a critical error\n\n## 5.4 TASK MANAGEMENT CYCLE\n1. STATE EVALUATION: Examine Todo.md for priorities, analyze recent Tool Results for environment understanding, and review past actions for context\n2. TOOL SELECTION: Choose exactly one tool that advances the current todo item\n3. EXECUTION: Wait for tool execution and observe results\n4. **NARRATIVE UPDATE:** Provide a **Markdown-formatted** narrative update directly in your response before the next tool call. Include explanations of what you\'ve done, what you\'re about to do, and why. Use headers, brief paragraphs, and formatting to enhance readability.\n5. PROGRESS TRACKING: Update todo.md with completed items and new tasks\n6. METHODICAL ITERATION: Repeat until section completion\n7. SECTION TRANSITION: Document completion and move to next section\n8. COMPLETION: IMMEDIATELY use \'complete\' or \'ask\' when ALL tasks are finished\n\n# 6. CONTENT CREATION\n\n## 6.1 WRITING GUIDELINES\n- Write content in continuous paragraphs using varied sentence lengths for engaging prose; avoid list formatting\n- Use prose and paragraphs by default; Returns list of (path, timestamp).\\"\\"\\"\\n    duration = get_video_info(str(video_path)).get(\\"duration\\", 0)\\n    if duration <= 0:\\n        duration = 600\\n\\n    extract_fps = 1.0 / interval_sec\\n    pattern = str(Path(output_dir) / \\"frame_%06d.jpg\\")\\n\\n    # Extract at original resolution for accurate bbox positioning\\n    cmd = [\\n        \\"ffmpeg\\", \\"-y\\", \\"-i\\", str(video_path),\\n        \\"-vf\\", f\\"fps={extract_fps:.4f}\\",\\n        \\"-q:v\\", \\"3\\",  # JPEG quality (good enough for OCR)\\n        pattern\\n    ]\\n    result = subprocess.run(cmd, capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=300)\\n    if result.returncode != 0:\\n        logger.error(f\\"Frame extraction failed: {result.stderr[-500:]}\\")\\n        return []\\n\\n    frames = sorted(Path(output_dir).glob(\\"frame_*.jpg\\"))\\n    output = [(f, i * interval_sec) for i, f in enumerate(frames) if i * interval_sec <= duration]\\n    logger.info(f\\"Extracted {len(output)} OCR frames\\")\\n    return output\\n\\n\\ndef extract_single_frame(video_path, timestamp, output_path):\\n    \\"\\"\\"Extract a single frame at original resolution for bg color sampling.\\"\\"\\"\\n    cmd = [\\n        \\"ffmpeg\\", \\"-y\\", \\"-ss\\", str(timestamp),\\n        \\"-i\\", str(video_path),\\n        \\"-frames:v\\", \\"1\\",\\n        \\"-q:v\\", \\"2\\",\\n        str(output_path)\\n    ]\\n    result = subprocess.run(cmd, capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=30)\\n    return result.returncode == 0\\n\\n\\n# \\u2500\\u2500 Smart frame dedup \\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\ndef deduplicate_frames(frame_list, sample_step=1):\\n    \\"\\"\\"Return indices of frames that differ from previous.\\"\\"\\"\\n    if len(frame_list) <= 10:\\n        return list(range(len(frame_list)))\\n\\n    keep = [0]\\n    prev_hash = None\\n\\n    for i in range(0, len(frame_list), sample_step):\\n        path = frame_list[i][0] if isinstance(frame_list[i], tuple) else frame_list[i]\\n        try:\\n            with Image.open(path) as img:\\n                thumb = img.resize((32, 32), Image.Resampling.BILINEAR).convert(\\"L\\")\\n                h = hashlib.md5(thumb.tobytes()).hexdigest()\\n            if prev_hash is None or h != prev_hash:\\n                keep.append(i)\\n                prev_hash = h\\n        except:\\n            keep.append(i)\\n\\n    if keep[-1] != len(frame_list) - 1:\\n        keep.append(len(frame_list) - 1)\\n\\n    return sorted(set(keep))\\n\\n\\n# \\u2500\\u2500 Region classification \\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\ndef classify_region(bbox, img_w, img_h):\\n    cx = (min(p[0] for p in bbox) + max(p[0] for p in bbox)) / 2\\n    cy = (min(p[1] for p in bbox) + max(p[1] for p in bbox)) / 2\\n    if img_h > img_w * 1.5:\\n        if cx < img_w * 0.15: return \\"LEFT_TOOLBAR\\"\\n        if cx > img_w * 0.70: return \\"RIGHT_PANEL\\"\\n        if cy < img_h * 0.06: return \\"TOP_BAR\\"\\n        if cy > img_h * 0.94: return \\"BOTTOM_BAR\\"\\n        return \\"CANVAS\\"\\n    else:\\n        if cx < img_w * 0.12: return \\"LEFT_TOOLBAR\\"\\n        if cx > img_w * 0.78: return \\"RIGHT_PANEL\\"\\n        if cy < img_h * 0.08: return \\"TOP_BAR\\"\\n        if cy > img_h * 0.92: return \\"BOTTOM_BAR\\"\\n        return \\"CANVAS\\"\\n\\n\\ndef filter_garbage(results):\\n    \\"\\"\\"Remove likely garbage/noise entries.\\"\\"\\"\\n    filtered = []\\n    for r in results:\\n        text = r.get(\\"text\\", \\"\\").strip()\\n        if not text: continue\\n        # Skip pure ellipsis/periods\\n        if re.match(r\'^[\\\\.\\\\u3002\\\\uff0e\\\\u2026\\\\s]+[!\\\\uff1f?!]*$\', text): continue\\n        # Skip very short text with low confidence\\n        if len(text) <= 2 and r.get(\\"confidence\\", 0) < 0.9: continue\\n        # Skip entries that are only punctuation and symbols\\n        if re.match(r\'^[^\\\\w\\\\u3040-\\\\u9fff]+$\', text): continue\\n        # Skip known Clip Studio Paint UI labels\\n        ui_noise = [\\n            \\"\\\\u30aa\\\\u30d7\\\\u30b7\\\\u30e7\\\\u30f3\\", \\"\\\\u30c4\\\\u30fc\\\\u30eb\\\\u30aa\\\\u30d7\\\\u30b7\\\\u30e7\\\\u30f3\\",\\n            \\"\\\\u9078\\\\u629e\\", \\"\\\\u30ec\\\\u30a4\\\\u30e4\\\\u30fc\\", \\"\\\\u30d7\\\\u30ed\\\\u30d1\\\\u30c6\\\\u30a3\\",\\n            \\"\\\\u30d6\\\\u30e9\\\\u30b7\\", \\"\\\\u30ab\\\\u30e9\\\\u30fc\\", \\"\\\\u30ad\\\\u30e3\\\\u30f3\\\\u30d0\\\\u30b9\\",\\n            \\"\\\\u30a6\\\\u30a3\\\\u30f3\\\\u30c9\\\\u30a6\\", \\"\\\\u30d5\\\\u30a3\\\\u30eb\\\\u30bf\\", \\"\\\\u30d8\\\\u30eb\\\\u30d7\\",\\n            \\"\\\\u7de8\\\\u96c6\\", \\"\\\\u8868\\\\u793a\\", \\"\\\\u30a2\\\\u30af\\\\u30b7\\\\u30e7\\\\u30f3\\",  # Action\\n            \\"\\\\u30da\\\\u30f3\\\\u30c4\\\\u30fc\\\\u30eb\\",  # Pen tool\\n            \\"\\\\u30d9\\\\u30f3\\\\u30c4\\\\u30fc\\\\u30eb\\",  # Pen tool variant\\n            \\"\\\\u30a4\\\\u30fc\\\\u30b8\\\\u30fc\\\\u30c4\\\\u30fc\\\\u30eb\\",  # Eraser tool\\n            \\"\\\\u30d0\\\\u30b1\\\\u30c4\\\\u30fc\\\\u30eb\\",  # Bucket tool\\n            \\"\\\\u30c6\\\\u30ad\\\\u30b9\\\\u30c8\\\\u30fc\\\\u30eb\\",  # Text tool\\n            \\"\\\\u30b0\\\\u30e9\\\\u30c7\\\\u30fc\\\\u30b7\\\\u30e7\\\\u30f3\\",  # Gradation\\n            \\"\\\\u30b5\\\\u30fc\\\\u30d5\\\\u30a7\\\\u30b9\\",  # Surface\\n            \\"\\\\u30d6\\\\u30ec\\\\u30f3\\\\u30c9\\\\u30e2\\\\u30fc\\\\u30c9\\",  # Blend mode\\n            \\"\\\\u4e0d\\\\u900f\\\\u660e\\\\u5ea6\\",  # Opacity\\n            \\"\\\\u63cf\\\\u753b\\\\u8272\\",  # Drawing color\\n            \\"\\\\u8272\\\\u9078\\\\u629e\\",  # Color selection\\n            \\"\\\\u30b3\\\\u30f3\\\\u30c8\\\\u30ed\\\\u30fc\\\\u30e9\\",  # Controller\\n            \\"\\\\u7dda\\\\u5e45\\\\u5909\\\\u66f4\\",  # Line width change\\n            \\"\\\\u30dd\\\\u30fc\\\\u30ba\\\\u30b9\\\\u30c8\\",  # Pose ST\\n            \\"\\\\u3082\\\\u3058\\",  # Character/text tool\\n        ]\\n        is_noise = any(p in text and len(text) <= len(p) + 4 for p in ui_noise)\\n        if is_noise: continue\\n        # Skip text that\'s mostly garbled (high ratio of single chars / non-Japanese)\\n        jp_chars = sum(1 for c in text if \'\\\\u3040\' <= c <= \'\\\\u9fff\' or \'\\\\uff00\' <= c <= \'\\\\uffef\')\\n        total_chars = len(text.replace(\' \', \'\'))\\n        if total_chars > 3 and jp_chars / total_chars < 0.3 and r.get(\\"confidence\\", 0) < 0.5:\\n            continue  # likely garbled OCR\\n        # Skip garbled katakana sequences (common OCR artifact from UI tool names)\\n        # These look like real words but are misread tool names\\n        katakana_only = re.sub(r\'[\\\\u30a1-\\\\u30ff\\\\uff66-\\\\uff9f\\\\u30fb\\\\u30fc\\\\u3000-\\\\u303f\\\\uff01-\\\\uff5e]\', \'\', text)\\n        if len(katakana_only) == 0 and len(text) <= 8 and r.get(\\"confidence\\", 0) < 0.6:\\n            # Very short all-katakana with low confidence = likely misread tool name\\n            continue\\n        # Skip entries from RIGHT_PANEL/LEFT_TOOLBAR with very low confidence\\n        region = r.get(\\"region\\", \\"\\")\\n        if region in (\\"RIGHT_PANEL\\", \\"LEFT_TOOLBAR\\", \\"TOP_BAR\\", \\"BOTTOM_BAR\\") and r.get(\\"confidence\\", 0) < 0.5:\\n            continue\\n        filtered.append(r)\\n    return filtered\\n\\n\\n# \\u2500\\u2500 OCR \\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\ndef run_ocr_on_frames(frame_paths, backend=\\"manga_ocr\\", lang=\\"ja\\",\\n                      video_path=None, orig_width=None, orig_height=None,\\n                      interval_sec=2.0):\\n    \\"\\"\\"Run OCR on selected frames.\\n\\n    The OCR frames may be downscaled. We need to scale bboxes back to\\n    original video resolution for accurate positioning.\\n\\n    Returns list of result dicts with:\\n      timestamp_sec, bbox (in original video coords), text, confidence, region\\n    \\"\\"\\"\\n    import easyocr\\n\\n    logger.info(\\"Initializing EasyOCR reader...\\")\\n    reader = easyocr.Reader([\\"ja\\", \\"en\\"], gpu=False, verbose=False)\\n\\n    manga_engine = None\\n    if backend == \\"manga_ocr\\":\\n        try:\\n            from manga_ocr import MangaOcr\\n            logger.info(\\"Initializing manga-ocr engine...\\")\\n            manga_engine = MangaOcr()\\n        except ImportError:\\n            logger.warning(\\"manga-ocr not available, using EasyOCR only\\")\\n            backend = \\"easyocr\\"\\n\\n    all_ocr = []\\n    ocr_width = None  # will be set from first frame\\n\\n    for idx, (frame_path, timestamp) in enumerate(frame_paths):\\n        logger.info(f\\"OCR frame {idx+1}/{len(frame_paths)}: ts={timestamp:.1f}s\\")\\n\\n        # Get OCR frame dimensions for scaling\\n        with Image.open(frame_path) as img:\\n            frame_w, frame_h = img.size\\n            if ocr_width is None:\\n                ocr_width = frame_w\\n\\n        # Scale factor: OCR frames may be downscaled\\n        scale_x = orig_width / frame_w if orig_width and frame_w else 1.0\\n        scale_y = orig_height / frame_h if orig_height and frame_h else 1.0\\n\\n        # Step 1: EasyOCR detection\\n        try:\\n            easy_results = reader.readtext(str(frame_path), paragraph=False)\\n        except Exception as e:\\n            logger.error(f\\"EasyOCR failed: {e}\\")\\n            continue\\n\\n        frame_results = []\\n        for bbox, text, confidence in easy_results:\\n            if not text.strip() or len(text.strip()) < MIN_TEXT_LEN:\\n                continue\\n\\n            # Calculate bbox dimensions for filtering\\n            bx1 = int(min(p[0] for p in bbox))\\n            by1 = int(min(p[1] for p in bbox))\\n            bx2 = int(max(p[0] for p in bbox))\\n            by2 = int(max(p[1] for p in bbox))\\n            bw = bx2 - bx1\\n            bh = by2 - by1\\n            barea = bw * bh\\n\\n            # Classify region first for confidence threshold\\n            temp_region = classify_region([[bx1, by1], [bx2, by1], [bx2, by2], [bx1, by2]],\\n                                          orig_width or frame_w, orig_height or frame_h)\\n\\n            # Lower confidence threshold for CANVAS text (important content)\\n            min_conf = CANVAS_CONFIDENCE if temp_region == \\"CANVAS\\" and barea > 2000 else MIN_CONFIDENCE\\n\\n            if confidence < min_conf:\\n                continue\\n\\n            # Skip very small bboxes (likely UI noise)\\n            if barea < MIN_BBOX_AREA:\\n                continue\\n\\n            # Scale bbox to original video resolution\\n            bbox_scaled = [[int(p[0] * scale_x), int(p[1] * scale_y)] for p in bbox]\\n\\n            result = {\\n                \\"bbox\\": bbox_scaled,\\n                \\"text\\": text.strip(),\\n                \\"confidence\\": round(float(confidence), 3),\\n                \\"timestamp_sec\\": round(timestamp, 2),\\n            }\\n\\n            # Step 2: manga-ocr refinement (only for CANVAS text, UI text is fine as-is)\\n            if manga_engine and backend == \\"manga_ocr\\" and temp_region == \\"CANVAS\\":\\n                try:\\n                    img = Image.open(frame_path)\\n                    x1 = int(min(p[0] for p in bbox))\\n                    y1 = int(min(p[1] for p in bbox))\\n                    x2 = int(max(p[0] for p in bbox))\\n                    y2 = int(max(p[1] for p in bbox))\\n                    \\n                    # Only run manga-ocr if the bbox has a reasonable aspect ratio\\n                    # (width > height * 2 \\u2014 text is typically wider than tall)\\n                    # Very tall bboxes likely include drawing content that confuses manga-ocr\\n                    aspect = (x2 - x1) / max(1, (y2 - y1))\\n                    \\n                    if aspect >= 1.5:\\n                        # Good aspect ratio for text \\u2014 run manga-ocr with padding\\n                        pad = max(5, int(min(x2 - x1, y2 - y1) * 0.08))\\n                        crop = img.crop((\\n                            max(0, x1 - pad), max(0, y1 - pad),\\n                            min(img.width, x2 + pad), min(img.height, y2 + pad)\\n                        ))\\n                        refined = manga_engine(crop)\\n                        \\n                        if refined.strip() and len(refined.strip()) >= len(text.strip()) * 0.5:\\n                            # Check if manga-ocr result is more coherent\\n                            # (contains more Japanese characters than the EasyOCR result)\\n                            easy_jp = sum(1 for c in text if \'\\\\u3040\' <= c <= \'\\\\u9fff\')\\n                            manga_jp = sum(1 for c in refined if \'\\\\u3040\' <= c <= \'\\\\u9fff\')\\n                            if manga_jp >= easy_jp * 0.8:\\n                                result[\\"text\\"] = refined.strip()\\n                                result[\\"confidence\\"] = max(result[\\"confidence\\"], 0.75)\\n                    else:\\n                        # Bad aspect ratio \\u2014 try splitting the bbox into horizontal strips\\n                        # and running manga-ocr on each strip\\n                        strip_height = (y2 - y1) // 2\\n                        strips_text = []\\n                        for sy in range(y1, y2, max(strip_height, 20)):\\n                            sy_end = min(sy + strip_height + 5, y2)\\n                            strip_crop = img.crop((\\n                                max(0, x1 - 3), max(0, sy - 3),\\n                                min(img.width, x2 + 3), min(img.height, sy_end + 3)\\n                            ))\\n                            strip_text = manga_engine(strip_crop)\\n                            if strip_text.strip() and not re.match(r\'^[\\\\.\\\\u3002\\\\uff0e\\\\u2026\\\\s]+$\', strip_text):\\n                                strips_text.append(strip_text.strip())\\n                        \\n                        if strips_text:\\n                            combined = \' \'.join(strips_text)\\n                            if len(combined) >= len(text.strip()) * 0.5:\\n                                result[\\"text\\"] = combined\\n                                result[\\"confidence\\"] = max(result[\\"confidence\\"], 0.75)\\n                    \\n                    img.close()\\n                except Exception as e:\\n                    logger.debug(f\\"manga-ocr refinement failed: {e}\\")\\n\\n            # Classify region (using original video coords)\\n            result[\\"region\\"] = classify_region(result[\\"bbox\\"],\\n                                               orig_width or frame_w,\\n                                               orig_height or frame_h)\\n\\n            frame_results.append(result)\\n\\n        if frame_results:\\n            frame_results = filter_garbage(frame_results)\\n            all_ocr.extend(frame_results)\\n\\n    # Deduplicate: merge same text at similar positions across timestamps\\n    all_ocr = deduplicate_ocr_results(all_ocr, interval_sec=2.0)\\n\\n    logger.info(f\\"OCR found {len(all_ocr)} text regions total (after dedup)\\")\\n    return all_ocr\\n\\n\\ndef deduplicate_ocr_results(results, interval_sec=2.0):\\n    \\"\\"\\"Merge same-text detections at similar positions into single entries\\n    with expanded time ranges.\\"\\"\\"\\n    if not results:\\n        return results\\n\\n    # Sort by timestamp\\n    results.sort(key=lambda r: r[\\"timestamp_sec\\"])\\n\\n    merged = []\\n    for r in results:\\n        # Check if this result overlaps with an existing merged entry\\n        found_merge = False\\n        for m in merged:\\n            same_text = r[\\"text\\"] == m[\\"text\\"]\\n            close_position = bbox_overlap(r[\\"bbox\\"], m[\\"bbox\\"]) > 0.3\\n            close_time = abs(r[\\"timestamp_sec\\"] - m[\\"timestamp_sec\\"]) < interval_sec * 3\\n\\n            if same_text and close_position and close_time:\\n                # Expand time range\\n                m[\\"timestamp_sec\\"] = min(m[\\"timestamp_sec\\"], r[\\"timestamp_sec\\"])\\n                m[\\"end_sec\\"] = max(m.get(\\"end_sec\\", m[\\"timestamp_sec\\"] + interval_sec),\\n                                   r[\\"timestamp_sec\\"] + interval_sec)\\n                # Use higher confidence\\n                m[\\"confidence\\"] = max(m[\\"confidence\\"], r[\\"confidence\\"])\\n                found_merge = True\\n                break\\n\\n        if not found_merge:\\n            r_copy = dict(r)\\n            r_copy[\\"end_sec\\"] = r[\\"timestamp_sec\\"] + interval_sec\\n            merged.append(r_copy)\\n\\n    return merged\\n\\n\\ndef bbox_overlap(bbox_a, bbox_b):\\n    \\"\\"\\"Compute IoU-like overlap between two bboxes.\\"\\"\\"\\n    try:\\n        ax1, ay1 = min(p[0] for p in bbox_a), min(p[1] for p in bbox_a)\\n        ax2, ay2 = max(p[0] for p in bbox_a), max(p[1] for p in bbox_a)\\n        bx1, by1 = min(p[0] for p in bbox_b), min(p[1] for p in bbox_b)\\n        bx2, by2 = max(p[0] for p in bbox_b), max(p[1] for p in bbox_b)\\n        ix1 = max(ax1, bx1)\\n        iy1 = max(ay1, by1)\\n        ix2 = min(ax2, bx2)\\n        iy2 = min(ay2, by2)\\n        if ix2 <= ix1 or iy2 <= iy1:\\n            return 0.0\\n        inter = (ix2 - ix1) * (iy2 - iy1)\\n        area_a = (ax2 - ax1) * (ay2 - ay1)\\n        area_b = (bx2 - bx1) * (by2 - by1)\\n        union = area_a + area_b - inter\\n        return inter / union if union > 0 else 0.0\\n    except (IndexError, TypeError):\\n        return 0.0\\n\\n\\n# \\u2500\\u2500 Translation \\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\u2500\\ndef translate_texts(ocr_results, src_lang=\\"ja\\", dst_lang=\\"en\\"):\\n    \\"\\"\\"Translate all unique OCR texts.\\"\\"\\"\\n    try:\\n        from deep_translator import GoogleTranslator\\n    except ImportError:\\n        logger.error(\\"deep-translator not installed!\\")\\n        return {}\\n\\n    translator = GoogleTranslator(source=src_lang, target=dst_lang)\\n\\n    unique_texts = set(r[\\"text\\"] for r in ocr_results)\\n    logger.info(f\\"Translating {len(unique_texts)} unique text segments...\\")\\n\\n    translations = {}\\n    for text in sorted(unique_texts):\\n        try:\\n            translated = translator.translate(text)\\n            if translated:\\n                translations[text] = translated\\n                logger.info(f\\"  {text} -> {translated}\\")\\n            else:\\n                translations[text] = text\\n        except Exception as e:\\n            logger.warning(f\\"Translation failed for \'{text}\': {e}\\")\\n {'role': 'tool', 'content': '{"output": "#!/usr/bin/env python3\\n\\"\\"\\"Enhanced OCR with text enlargement for small UI text.\\n\\nThis module provides the OCR pipeline that:\\n1. Detects text regions with EasyOCR\\n2. For small/low-confidence regions: enlarges, enhances, and re-OCR\'s\\n3. Uses manga-ocr for Japanese text recognition on enlarged crops\\n4. Returns accurate results with proper bounding boxes\\n\\"\\"\\"\\n\\nimport logging\\nimport re\\nfrom pathlib import Path\\nfrom typing import Any\\n\\nfrom PIL import Image, ImageEnhance, ImageFilter\\n\\nlogger = logging.getLogger(\\"enhanced_ocr\\")\\n\\n# Minimum sizes below which we enlarge text for better OCR\\nENLARGE_THRESHOLD_WIDTH = 150   # pixels - text narrower than this gets enlarged\\nENLARGE_THRESHOLD_HEIGHT = 40   # pixels - text shorter than this gets enlarged\\nENLARGE_FACTOR = 3              # how much to enlarge small text\\nENHANCE_SHARPNESS = 2.0        # sharpening factor for enlarged text\\nENHANCE_CONTRAST = 1.5         # contrast enhancement factor\\n\\n\\ndef enlarge_and_enhance(image_crop: Image.Image, factor: int = ENLARGE_FACTOR) -> Image.Image:\\n    \\"\\"\\"Enlarge a text crop and enhance it for better OCR.\\n    \\n    Steps:\\n    1. Upscale by factor using high-quality resampling\\n    2. Convert to grayscale\\n    3. Increase contrast\\n    4. Sharpen\\n    5. Apply threshold to get clean black/white text\\n    \\"\\"\\"\\n    # Upscale\\n    new_w = image_crop.width * factor\\n    new_h = image_crop.height * factor\\n    enlarged = image_crop.resize((new_w, new_h), Image.Resampling.LANCZOS)\\n    \\n    # Convert to grayscale\\n    gray = enlarged.convert(\\"L\\")\\n    \\n    # Enhance contrast\\n    enhancer = ImageEnhance.Contrast(gray)\\n    gray = enhancer.enhance(ENHANCE_CONTRAST)\\n    \\n    # Sharpen\\n    enhancer = ImageEnhance.Sharpness(gray)\\n    gray = enhancer.enhance(ENHANCE_SHARPNESS)\\n    \\n    # Apply threshold: make it nearly binary (black text on white bg)\\n    # This helps OCR engines tremendously\\n    threshold = 128\\n    binary = gray.point(lambda x: 255 if x > threshold else 0, \'1\')\\n    # Convert back to RGB for OCR engines that expect it\\n    result = binary.convert(\\"RGB\\")\\n    \\n    return result\\n\\n\\ndef should_enlarge(bbox_width: int, bbox_height: int, confidence: float) -> bool:\\n    \\"\\"\\"Determine if a text region should be enlarged for better OCR.\\"\\"\\"\\n    # Small regions always need enlargement\\n    if bbox_width < ENLARGE_THRESHOLD_WIDTH or bbox_height < ENLARGE_THRESHOLD_HEIGHT:\\n        return True\\n    # Low confidence medium regions benefit from enlargement\\n    if confidence < 0.6 and (bbox_width < ENLARGE_THRESHOLD_WIDTH * 2 or \\n                              bbox_height < ENLARGE_THRESHOLD_HEIGHT * 2):\\n        return True\\n    return False\\n\\n\\ndef ocr_with_enlargement(\\n    frame_image: Image.Image,\\n    easyocr_reader: Any,\\n    manga_ocr_engine: Any = None,\\n    min_confidence: float = 0.3,\\n    min_text_len: int = 2,\\n    min_bbox_area: int = 300,\\n    img_width: int = 0,\\n    img_height: int = 0,\\n) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:\\n    \\"\\"\\"Run OCR with text enlargement for small/low-confidence regions.\\n    \\n    Pipeline:\\n    1. EasyOCR detection on full frame\\n    2. For each detected region:\\n       a. If small or low-confidence: crop, enlarge, enhance, re-OCR\\n       b. If large and high-confidence: use EasyOCR result directly\\n    3. For Japanese text: use manga-ocr on enlarged crops for better recognition\\n    4. Classify UI region\\n    5. Filter garbage\\n    \\"\\"\\"\\n    \\n    # Step 1: EasyOCR detection on full frame\\n    try:\\n        easy_results = easyocr_reader.readtext(str(frame_image.filename) if hasattr(frame_image, \'filename\') else None, paragraph=False)\\n    except Exception as e:\\n        logger.error(f\\"EasyOCR detection failed: {e}\\")\\n        #     \\"/usr/share/fonts/truetype/dejavu/DejaVuSans-Bold.ttf\\",\\n    ]\\n    for path in candidates:\\n        if os.path.exists(path):\\n            return path\\n    for root, dirs, files in timeout=120)\\n    subprocess.run([\\"apt-get\\", \\"install\\", \\"-y\\", \\"fonts-dejavu-core\\"],\\n                    capture_output=True, timeout=60)\\n\\n\\n# ── Video info ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\\ndef get_video_info(video_path):\\n    cmd = [\\"ffprobe\\", \\"-v\\", \\"quiet\\", \\"-print_format\\", \\"json\\",\\n           \\"-show_streams\\", \\"-show_format\\", str(video_path)]\\n    result = subprocess.run(cmd, capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=30)\\n    try:\\n        info = json.loads(result.stdout)\\n        vs = next((s for s in info.get(\\"streams\\", [])\\n                    if s.get(\\"codec_type\\") == \\"video\\"), {})\\n        fps_str = vs.get(\\"r_frame_rate\\", \\"30/1\\")\\n        if \\"/\\" in fps_str:\\n            num, den = fps_str.split(\\"/\\")\\n            fps = float(num) / float(den)\\n        else:\\n            fps = float(fps_str)\\n        return {\\n            \\"width\\": int(vs.get(\\"width\\", 0)),\\n            \\"height\\": int(vs.get(\\"height\\", 0)),\\n            \\"duration\\": float(info.get(\\"format\\", {}).get(\\"duration\\", 0)),\\n            \\"fps\\": fps,\\n        }\\n    except:\\n        return {}\\n\\n\\n# ── Frame extraction (for OCR only, small JPEGs) ───────────────────────────\\ndef extract_ocr_frames(video_path, output_dir, interval_sec=2.0):\\n    \\"\\"\\"Extract frames at intervals for OCR. Returns list of (path, timestamp).\\"\\"\\"\\n    duration = get_video_info(str(video_path)).get(\\"duration\\", 0)\\n    if duration <= 0:\\n        duration = 600\\n\\n    extract_fps = 1.0 / interval_sec\\n    pattern = str(Path(output_dir) / \\"frame_%06d.jpg\\")\\n\\n    cmd = [\\n        \\"ffmpeg\\", \\"-y\\", \\"-i\\", str(video_path),\\n        \\"-vf\\", f\\"fps={extract_fps:.4f}\\",\\n        \\"-q:v\\", \\"3\\",\\n        pattern\\n    ]\\n    result = subprocess.run(cmd, capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=300)\\n    if result.returncode != 0:\\n        logger.error(f\\"Frame extraction failed: {result.stderr[-500:]}\\")\\n        return []\\n\\n    frames = sorted(Path(output_dir).glob(\\"frame_*.jpg\\"))\\n    output = [(f, i * interval_sec) for i, f in enumerate(frames) if i * interval_sec <= duration]\\n    logger.info(f\\"Extracted {len(output)} OCR frames\\")\\n    return output\\n\\n\\ndef extract_single_frame(video_path, timestamp, output_path):\\n    \\"\\"\\"Extract a single frame at original resolution for bg color sampling.\\"\\"\\"\\n    cmd = [\\n        \\"ffmpeg\\", \\"-y\\", \\"-ss\\", str(timestamp),\\n        \\"-i\\", str(video_path),\\n        \\"-frames:v\\", \\"1\\",\\n        \\"-q:v\\", \\"2\\",\\n        str(output_path)\\n    ]\\n    result = subprocess.run(cmd, capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=30)\\n    return result.returncode == 0\\n\\n\\n# ── Smart frame dedup ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────\\ndef deduplicate_frames(frame_list, sample_step=1):\\n    \\"\\"\\"Return indices of frames that differ from previous.\\"\\"\\"\\n    if len(frame_list) <= 10:\\n        return list(range(len(frame_list)))\\n\\n    keep = [0]\\n    prev_hash = None\\n\\n    for i in range(0, len(frame_list), sample_step):\\n        path = frame_list[i][0] if isinstance(frame_list[i], tuple) else frame_list[i]\\n        try:\\n            with Image.open(path) as img:\\n                thumb = img.resize((32, 32), Image.Resampling.BILINEAR).convert(\\"L\\")\\n                h = hashlib.md5(thumb.tobytes()).hexdigest()\\n            if prev_hash is None or h != prev_hash:\\n                keep.append(i)\\n                prev_hash = h\\n        except:\\n            keep.append(i)\\n\\n    if keep[-1] != len(frame_list) - 1:\\n        keep.append(len(frame_list) - 1)\\n\\n    return sorted(set(keep))\\n\\n\\n# ── Region classification ──────────────────────────────────────────────────\\ndef classify_region(bbox, img_w, img_h):\\n    cx = (min(p[0] for p in bbox) + max(p[0] for p in bbox)) / 2\\n    cy = (min(p[1] for p in bbox) + max(p[1] for p in bbox)) / 2\\n    if img_h > img_w * 1.5:\\n        if cx < img_w * 0.15: return \\"LEFT_TOOLBAR\\"\\n        if cx > img_w * 0.70: return \\"RIGHT_PANEL\\"\\n        if cy < img_h * 0.06: return \\"TOP_BAR\\"\\n        if cy > img_h * 0.94: return \\"BOTTOM_BAR\\"\\n        return \\"CANVAS\\"\\n    else:\\n        if cx < img_w * 0.12: return \\"LEFT_TOOLBAR\\"\\n        if cx > img_w * 0.78: return \\"RIGHT_PANEL\\"\\n        if cy < img_h * 0.08: return \\"TOP_BAR\\"\\n        if cy > img_h * 0.92: return \\"BOTTOM_BAR\\"\\n        return \\"CANVAS\\"\\n\\n\\n# ── Text enlargement ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\\ndef enlarge_and_enhance(image_crop, factor=ENLARGE_FACTOR):\\n    \\"\\"\\"Enlarge a text crop and enhance it for better OCR.\\n\\n    Steps: upscale → grayscale → contrast → sharpen → threshold → RGB\\n    \\"\\"\\"\\n    new_w = image_crop.width * factor\\n    new_h = image_crop.height * factor\\n    enlarged = image_crop.resize((new_w, new_h), Image.Resampling.LANCZOS)\\n\\n    gray = enlarged.convert(\\"L\\")\\n    enhancer = ImageEnhance.Contrast(gray)\\n    gray = enhancer.enhance(ENHANCE_CONTRAST)\\n    enhancer = ImageEnhance.Sharpness(gray)\\n    gray = enhancer.enhance(ENHANCE_SHARPNESS)\\n\\n    # Threshold to binary (clean black text on white background)\\n    threshold = 128\\n    binary = gray.point(lambda x: 255 if x > threshold else 0, \'1\')\\n    result = binary.convert(\\"RGB\\")\\n    return result\\n\\n\\ndef should_enlarge(bbox_w, bbox_h, confidence):\\n    \\"\\"\\"Determine if a text region should be enlarged for better OCR.\\"\\"\\"\\n    if bbox_w < ENLARGE_THRESHOLD_WIDTH or bbox_h < ENLARGE_THRESHOLD_HEIGHT:\\n        return True\\n    if confidence < 0.6 and (bbox_w < ENLARGE_THRESHOLD_WIDTH * 2 or\\n                              bbox_h < ENLARGE_THRESHOLD_HEIGHT * 2):\\n        return True\\n    return False\\n\\n\\n# ── Garbage filter ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\\ndef filter_garbage(results):\\n    \\"\\"\\"Remove likely garbage/noise entries from OCR results.\\n\\n    Now less aggressive: UI labels are kept (they\'ll be translated via\\n    UI_LABEL_DICT or Google Translate). Only truly garbled OCR is removed.\\n    \\"\\"\\"\\n    filtered = []\\n    for r in results:\\n        text = r.get(\\"text\\", \\"\\").strip()\\n        if not text:\\n            continue\\n\\n        # Skip pure ellipsis/periods\\n        if re.match(r\'^[\\\\.。\\\\u2026\\\\s]+[!？！]*$\', text):\\n            continue\\n\\n        # Skip very short text with low confidence (but NOT if it\'s a known UI label)\\n        if len(text) <= 2 and r.get(\\"confidence\\", 0) < 0.9:\\n            if _is_ui_label(text) is None:\\n                continue\\n\\n        # Skip entries that are only punctuation and symbols\\n        if re.match(r\'^[^\\\\w\\\\u3040-\\\\u9fff]+$\', text):\\n            continue\\n\\n        # Check if it\'s a known UI label — always keep these\\n        if _is_ui_label(text) is not None:\\n            filtered.append(r)\\n            continue\\n\\n        # Skip text with very low Japanese character ratio (garbled OCR)\\n        jp_chars = sum(1 for c in text if \'\\\\u3040\' <= c <= \'\\\\u9fff\' or \'\\\\uff00\' <= c <= \'\\\\uffef\')\\n        total_chars = len(text.replace(\' \', \'\'))\\n        if total_chars > 4 and jp_chars / total_chars < 0.3 and r.get(\\"confidence\\", 0) < 0.4:\\n            continue\\n\\n        # Skip garbled katakana sequences with low confidence\\n        katakana_only = re.sub(r\'[\\\\u30a1-\\\\u30ff\\\\uff66-\\\\uff9f\\\\u30fb\\\\u30fc\\\\u3000-\\\\u303f\\\\uff01-\\\\uff5e]\', \'\', text)\\n        if len(katakana_only) == 0 and len(text) <= 10 and r.get(\\"confidence\\", 0) < 0.5:\\n            continue\\n\\n        # Skip UI panel text with very low confidence (but higher threshold than before)\\n        region = r.get(\\"region\\", \\"\\")\\n        if region in (\\"RIGHT_PANEL\\", \\"LEFT_TOOLBAR\\", \\"TOP_BAR\\", \\"BOTTOM_BAR\\"):\\n            if r.get(\\"confidence\\", 0) < 0.35:\\n                continue\\n\\n        filtered.append(r)\\n    return filtered\\n\\n\\n# ── OCR with enlargement ────────────────────────────────────────────────────\\ndef run_ocr_on_frames(frame_paths, backend=\\"manga_ocr\\", lang=\\"ja\\",\\n                      video_path=None, orig_width=None, orig_height=None,\\n                      interval_sec=2.0):\\n    \\"\\"\\"Run OCR on selected frames with text enlargement for small UI text.\\n\\n    Pipeline per frame:\\n    1. EasyOCR detection on full frame\\n    2. For each detected region:\\n       a. Classify region (CANVAS, LEFT_TOOLBAR, RIGHT_PANEL, etc.)\\n       b. If small/low-confidence: crop, enlarge 3x, enhance, re-OCR\\n       c. If large CANVAS text: try manga-ocr on cropped region\\n    3. For enlarged regions: try manga-ocr first, then EasyOCR on enlarged\\n    4. Apply garbage filter\\n    5. Deduplicate across timestamps\\n    \\"\\"\\"\\n    import easyocr\\n\\n    logger.info(\\"Initializing EasyOCR reader...\\")\\n    reader = easyocr.Reader([\\"ja\\", \\"en\\"], gpu=False, verbose=False)\\n\\n    manga_engine = None\\n    if backend == \\"manga_ocr\\":\\n        try:\\n            from manga_ocr import MangaOcr\\n            logger.info(\\"Initializing manga-ocr engine...\\")\\n            manga_engine = MangaOcr()\\n        except ImportError:\\n            logger.warning(\\"manga-ocr not available, using EasyOCR only\\")\\n            backend = \\"easyocr\\"\\n\\n    all_ocr = []\\n    ocr_width = None\\n\\n    for idx, (frame_path, timestamp) in enumerate(frame_paths):\\n        logger.info(f\\"OCR frame {idx+1}/{len(frame_paths)}: ts={timestamp:.1f}s\\")\\n\\n        with Image.open(frame_path) as img:\\n            frame_w, frame_h = img.size\\n            if ocr_width is None:\\n                ocr_width = frame_w\\n\\n        scale_x = orig_width / frame_w if orig_width and frame_w else 1.0\\n        scale_y = orig_height / frame_h if orig_height and frame_h else 1.0\\n\\n        # Step 1: EasyOCR detection\\n        try:\\n            easy_results = reader.readtext(str(frame_path), paragraph=False)\\n        except Exception as e:\\n            logger.error(f\\"EasyOCR failed: {e}\\")\\n            continue\\n\\n        frame_results = []\\n\\n        # Open image once for all crops\\n        frame_image = Image.open(frame_path)\\n\\n        for bbox, text, confidence in easy_results:\\n            if not text.strip() or len(text.strip()) < MIN_TEXT_LEN:\\n                continue\\n\\n            bx1 = int(min(p[0] for p in bbox))\\n            by1 = int(min(p[1] for p in bbox))\\n            bx2 = int(max(p[0] for p in bbox))\\n            by2 = int(max(p[1] for p in bbox))\\n            bw = bx2 - bx1\\n            bh = by2 - by1\\n            barea = bw * bh\\n\\n            # Classify region first\\n            temp_region = classify_region(\\n                [[bx1, by1], [bx2, by1], [bx2, by2], [bx1, by2]],\\n                orig_width or frame_w, orig_height or frame_h\\n            )\\n\\n            # Lower confidence threshold for CANVAS text\\n            min_conf = CANVAS_CONFIDENCE if temp_region == \\"CANVAS\\" and barea > 2000 else MIN_CONFIDENCE\\n            if confidence < min_conf:\\n                continue\\n\\n            # Minimum bbox area (lowered for UI text)\\n            if barea < MIN_BBOX_AREA:\\n                continue\\n\\n            # Scale bbox to original video resolution\\n            bbox_scaled = [[int(p[0] * scale_x), int(p[1] * scale_y)] for p in bbox]\\n\\n            result = {\\n                \\"bbox\\": bbox_scaled,\\n                \\"text\\": text.strip(),\\n                \\"confidence\\": round(float(confidence), 3),\\n                \\"timestamp_sec\\": round(timestamp, 2),\\n                \\"region\\": temp_region,\\n                \\"enlarged\\": False,\\n            }\\n\\n            # ── Text enlargement pipeline for small/low-confidence text ──\\n            if should_enlarge(bw, bh, confidence) and manga_engine is not None:\\n                try:\\n                    # Crop with padding\\n                    pad = max(5, int(min(bw, bh) * 0.1))\\n                    crop_box = (\\n                        max(0, bx1 - pad),\\n                        max(0, by1 - pad),\\n                        min(frame_image.width, bx2 + pad),\\n                        min(frame_image.height, by2 + pad),\\n                    )\\n                    crop = frame_image.crop(crop_box)\\n\\n                    # Enlarge and enhance\\n                    enlarged = enlarge_and_enhance(crop)\\n                    result[\\"enlarged\\"] = True\\n\\n                    # Try manga-ocr on the enlarged crop (best for Japanese)\\n                    manga_text = manga_engine(enlarged)\\n                    if manga_text.strip() and not re.match(r\'^[\\\\.。\\\\u2026\\\\s]+$\', manga_text):\\n                        # Validate: manga-ocr result should have decent Japanese char ratio\\n                        manga_jp = sum(1 for c in manga_text if \'\\\\u3040\' <= c <= \'\\\\u9fff\')\\n                        manga_total = len(manga_text.replace(\' \', \'\'))\\n                        if manga_total > 0 and manga_jp / manga_total >= 0.3:\\n                            result[\\"text\\"] = manga_text.strip()\\n                            result[\\"confidence\\"] = max(result[\\"confidence\\"], 0.75)\\n                            logger.debug(f\\"manga-ocr (enlarged): \'{text.strip()}\' -> \'{manga_text.strip()}\'\\")\\n                        else:\\n                            # manga-ocr returned non-Japanese garbage on enlarged crop\\n                            # Try EasyOCR on the enlarged crop\\n                            try:\\n                                enlarged_results = reader.readtext(enlarged, paragraph=False)\\n                                if enlarged_results:\\n                                    best = max(enlarged_results, key=lambda x: x[2])\\n                                    if best[2] > confidence and best[1].strip():\\n                                        result[\\"text\\"] = best[1].strip()\\n                                        result[\\"confidence\\"] = round(float(best[2]), 3)\\n                                        logger.debug(f\\"EasyOCR (enlarged): \'{text.strip()}\' -> \'{best[1].strip()}\'\\")\\n                            except:\\n                                pass\\n                    else:\\n                        # manga-ocr returned nothing useful on enlarged crop\\n                        # Try EasyOCR on enlarged crop\\n                        try:\\n                            enlarged_results = reader.readtext(enlarged, paragraph=False)\\n                            if enlarged_results:\\n                                best = max(enlarged_results, key=lambda x: x[2])\\n                                if best[2] > confidence and best[1].strip():\\n                                    result[\\"text\\"] = best[1].strip()\\n                                    result[\\"confidence\\"] = round(float(best[2]), 3)\\n                        except:\\n                            pass\\n                except Exception as e:\\n                    logger.debug(f\\"Enlargement pipeline failed: {e}\\")\\n\\n            # ── manga-ocr refinement for large CANVAS text (no enlargement needed) ──\\n            elif manga_engine and backend == \\"manga_ocr\\" and temp_region == \\"CANVAS\\":\\n                try:\\n                    aspect = bw / max(1, bh)\\n\\n                    if aspect >= 1.5:\\n                        # Good aspect ratio — run manga-ocr with padding\\n                        pad = max(5, int(min(bw, bh) * 0.08))\\n                        crop = frame_image.crop((\\n                            max(0, bx1 - pad), max(0, by1 - pad),\\n                            min(frame_image.width, bx2 + pad), min(frame_image.height, by2 + pad)\\n                        ))\\n                        refined = manga_engine(crop)\\n\\n                        if refined.strip() and len(refined.strip()) >= len(text.strip()) * 0.5:\\n                            easy_jp = sum(1 for c in text if \'\\\\u3040\' <= c <= \'\\\\u9fff\')\\n                            manga_jp = sum(1 for c in refined if \'\\\\u3040\' <= c <= \'\\\\u9fff\')\\n                            if manga_jp >= easy_jp * 0.8:\\n                                result[\\"text\\"] = refined.strip()\\n                                result[\\"confidence\\"] = max(result[\\"confidence\\"], 0.75)\\n                    else:\\n                        # Bad aspect ratio — try splitting into horizontal strips\\n                        strip_height = (by2 - by1) // 2\\n                        strips_text = []\\n                        for sy in range(by1, by2, max(strip_height, 20)):\\n                            sy_end = min(sy + strip_height + 5, by2)\\n                            strip_crop = frame_image.crop((\\n                                max(0, bx1 - 3), max(0, sy - 3),\\n                                min(frame_image.width, bx2 + 3), min(frame_image.height, sy_end + 3)\\n                            ))\\n                            strip_text = manga_engine(strip_crop)\\n                            if strip_text.strip() and not re.match(r\'^[\\\\.。\\\\u2026\\\\s]+$\', strip_text):\\n                                strips_text.append(strip_text.strip())\\n\\n                        if strips_text:\\n                            combined = \' \'.join(strips_text)\\n                            if len(combined) >= len(text.strip()) * 0.5:\\n                                result[\\"text\\"] = combined\\n                                result[\\"confidence\\"] = max(result[\\"confidence\\"], 0.75)\\n                except Exception as e:\\n                    logger.debug(f\\"manga-ocr refinement failed: {e}\\")\\n\\n            frame_results.append(result)\\n\\n        frame_image.close()\\n\\n        if frame_results:\\n            frame_results = filter_garbage(frame_results)\\n            all_ocr.extend(frame_results)\\n\\n    # Deduplicate\\n    all_ocr = deduplicate_ocr_results(all_ocr, interval_sec=2.0)\\n\\n    logger.info(f\\"OCR found {len(all_ocr)} text regions total (after dedup)\\")\\n    return all_ocr\\n\\n\\ndef deduplicate_ocr_results(results, interval_sec=2.0):\\n    \\"\\"\\"Merge same-text detections at similar positions into single entries.\\"\\"\\"\\n    if not results:\\n        return results\\n\\n    results.sort(key=lambda r: r[\\"timestamp_sec\\"])\\n\\n    merged = []\\n    for r in results:\\n        found_merge = False\\n        for m in merged:\\n            same_text = r[\\"text\\"] == m[\\"text\\"]\\n            close_position = bbox_overlap(r[\\"bbox\\"], m[\\"bbox\\"]) > 0.3\\n            close_time = abs(r[\\"timestamp_sec\\"] - m[\\"timestamp_sec\\"]) < interval_sec * 3\\n\\n            if same_text and close_position and close_time:\\n                m[\\"timestamp_sec\\"] = min(m[\\"timestamp_sec\\"], r[\\"timestamp_sec\\"])\\n                m[\\"end_sec\\"] = max(m.get(\\"end_sec\\", m[\\"timestamp_sec\\"] + interval_sec),\\n                                   r[\\"timestamp_sec\\"] + interval_sec)\\n                m[\\"confidence\\"] = max(m[\\"confidence\\"], r[\\"confidence\\"])\\n                found_merge = True\\n                break\\n\\n        if not found_merge:\\n            r_copy = dict(r)\\n            r_copy[\\"end_sec\\"] = r[\\"timestamp_sec\\"] + interval_sec\\n            merged.append(r_copy)\\n\\n    return merged\\n\\n\\ndef bbox_overlap(bbox_a, bbox_b):\\n    \\"\\"\\"Compute IoU-like overlap between two bboxes.\\"\\"\\"\\n    try:\\n        ax1, ay1 = min(p[0] for p in bbox_a), min(p[1] for p in bbox_a)\\n        ax2, ay2 = max(p[0] for p in bbox_a), max(p[1] for p in bbox_a)\\n        bx1, by1 = min(p[0] for p in bbox_b), min(p[1] for p in bbox_b)\\n        bx2, by2 = max(p[0] for p in bbox_b), max(p[1] for p in bbox_b)\\n        ix1 = max(ax1, bx1)\\n        iy1 = max(ay1, by1)\\n        ix2 = min(ax2, bx2)\\n        iy2 = min(ay2, by2)\\n        if ix2 <= ix1 or iy2 <= iy1:\\n            return 0.0\\n        inter = (ix2 - ix1) * (iy2 - iy1)\\n        area_a = (ax2 - ax1) * (ay2 - ay1)\\n        area_b = (bx2 - bx1) * (by2 - by1)\\n        union = area_a + area_b - inter\\n        return inter / union if union > 0 else 0.0\\n    except (IndexError, TypeError):\\n        return 0.0\\n\\n\\n# ── Translation ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\\ndef translate_texts(ocr_results, src_lang=\\"ja\\", dst_lang=\\"en\\"):\\n    \\"\\"\\"Translate all unique OCR texts.\\n\\n    Uses UI_LABEL_DICT for known UI labels, Google Translate for everything else.\\n    \\"\\"\\"\\n    try:\\n        from deep_translator import GoogleTranslator\\n    except ImportError:\\n        logger.error(\\"deep-translator not installed!\\")\\n        return {}\\n\\n    translator = GoogleTranslator(source=src_lang, target=dst_lang)\\n\\n    unique_texts = set(r[\\"text\\"] for r in ocr_results)\\n    logger.info(f\\"Translating {len(unique_texts)} unique text segments...\\")\\n\\n    translations = {}\\n    for text in sorted(unique_texts):\\n        # Check UI label dictionary first\\n        ui_translation = _is_ui_label(text)\\n        if ui_translation is not None:\\n            translations[text] = ui_translation\\n            logger.info(f\\"  [UI] {text} -> {ui_translation}\\")\\n            continue\\n\\n        # Google Translate for everything else\\n        try:\\n            translated = translator.translate(text)\\n            if translated:\\n                translations[text] = translated\\n                logger.info(f\\"  {text} -> {translated}\\")\\n            else:\\n                translations[text] = text\\n        except Exception as e:\\n            logger.warning(f\\"Translation failed for \'{text}\': {e}\\")\\n            translations[text] = text\\n\\n    return translations\\n\\n\\n# ── Background color sampling ────────────────────────────────────────────────\\ndef sample_bg_color(video_path, timestamp, bbox, padding=4):\\n    \\"\\"\\"Sample background color from around a text region in the video.\\"\\"\\"\\n    x1 = min(p[0] for p in bbox)\\n    y1 = min(p[1] for p in bbox)\\n    x2 = max(p[0] for p in bbox)\\n    y2 = max(p[1] for p in bbox)\\n\\n    with tempfile.NamedTemporaryFile(suffix=\\".png\\", delete=False) as tmp:\\n        tmp_path = tmp.name\\n\\n    if not extract_single_frame(video_path, timestamp, tmp_path):\\n        return \\"0x1a1a2e\\"\\n\\n    try:\\n        img = Image.open(tmp_path)\\n        w, h = img.size\\n        pixels = []\\n\\n        for dx in range(-padding, 0):\\n            for y in range(y1, y2, max(1, (y2 - y1) // 5)):\\n                px = x1 + dx\\n                if 0 <= px < w and 0 <= y < h:\\n                    try:\\n                        p = img.getpixel((px, y))\\n                        if isinstance(p, tuple) and len(p) >= 3:\\n                            pixels.append(p[:3])\\n                    except: pass\\n                px = x2 - dx - 1\\n                if 0 <= px < w and 0 <= y < h:\\n                    try:\\n                        p = img.getpixel((px, y))\\n                        if isinstance(p, tuple) and len(p) >= 3:\\n                            pixels.append(p[:3])\\n                    except: pass\\n\\n        for dy in range(-padding, 0):\\n            for x in range(x1, x2, max(1, (x2 - x1) // 5)):\\n                py = y1 + dy\\n                if 0 <= x < w and 0 <= py < h:\\n                    try:\\n                        p = img.getpixel((x, py))\\n                        if isinstance(p, tuple) and len(p) >= 3:\\n                            pixels.append(p[:3])\\n                    except: pass\\n                py = y2 - dy - 1\\n                if 0 <= x < w and 0 <= py < h:\\n                    try:\\n                        p = img.getpixel((x, py))\\n                        if isinstance(p, tuple) and len(p) >= 3:\\n                            pixels.append(p[:3])\\n                    except: pass\\n\\n        img.close()\\n        os.unlink(tmp_path)\\n\\n        if pixels:\\n            avg_r = sum(p[0] for p in pixels) // len(pixels)\\n            avg_g = sum(p[1] for p in pixels) // len(pixels)\\n            avg_b = sum(p[2] for p in pixels) // len(pixels)\\n            return f\\"0x{avg_r:02x}{avg_g:02x}{avg_b:02x}\\"\\n    except Exception as e:\\n        logger.debug(f\\"BG color sampling failed: {e}\\")\\n        try: os.unlink(tmp_path)\\n        except: pass\\n\\n    return \\"0x1a1a2e\\"\\n\\n\\n# ── Build ffmpeg filter chain ───────────────────────────────────────────────\\ndef build_ffmpeg_filters(ocr_results, translations, video_path, font_path,\\n                         interval_sec=2.0, canvas_only=False):\\n    \\"\\"\\"Build ffmpeg filter chain for inpainting + text overlay.\\"\\"\\"\\n    filters = []\\n    video_info = get_video_info(video_path)\\n    vid_w = video_info.get(\\"width\\", 1620)\\n    vid_h = video_info.get(\\"height\\", 748)\\n\\n    for r in ocr_results:\\n        if canvas_only and r.get(\\"region\\") != \\"CANVAS\\":\\n            continue\\n\\n        text = r[\\"text\\"]\\n        translated = translations.get(text, text)\\n\\n        # Skip if not Japanese and not translated\\n        if translated == text and not any(\'\\\\u3040\' <= c <= \'\\\\u9fff\' for c in text):\\n            continue\\n\\n        bbox = r[\\"bbox\\"]\\n        ts = r[\\"timestamp_sec\\"]\\n\\n        x1 = int(min(p[0] for p in bbox))\\n        y1 = int(min(p[1] for p in bbox))\\n        x2 = int(max(p[0] for p in bbox))\\n        y2 = int(max(p[1] for p in bbox))\\n        bbox_w = x2 - x1\\n        bbox_h = y2 - y1\\n\\n        if bbox_w <= 0 or bbox_h <= 0:\\n            continue\\n\\n        # Time window\\n        if \\"end_sec\\" in r:\\n            t_start = max(0, r[\\"timestamp_sec\\"] - interval_sec * 0.3)\\n            t_end = r[\\"end_sec\\"] + interval_sec * 0.3\\n        else:\\n            t_start = max(0, ts - interval_sec * 0.55)\\n            t_end = ts + interval_sec * 0.55\\n\\n        # ── Inpaint: drawbox to cover original text ──\\n        pad = INPAINT_PADDING\\n        ix1 = max(0, x1 - pad)\\n        iy1 = max(0, y1 - pad)\\n        ix2 = min(vid_w, x2 + pad)\\n        iy2 = min(vid_h, y2 + pad)\\n        iw = ix2 - ix1\\n        ih = iy2 - iy1\\n\\n        bg_color = sample_bg_color(video_path, ts, bbox, pad)\\n\\n        drawbox = (\\n            f\\"drawbox=x={ix1}:y={iy1}:w={iw}:h={ih}\\"\\n            f\\":color={bg_color}:t=fill\\"\\n            f\\":enable=\'between(t,{t_start:.2f},{t_end:.2f})\'\\"\\n        )\\n        filters.append(drawbox)\\n\\n        # ── Overlay: drawtext for English translation ──\\n        font_size = _calc_font_size(translated, bbox_w, bbox_h)\\n        safe_text = _escape_ffmpeg_text(translated)\\n        safe_font = font_path.replace(\\"\\\\\\\\\\", \\"\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\").replace(\\":\\", \\"\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\:\\")\\n\\n        drawtext = (\\n            f\\"drawtext=fontfile=\'{safe_font}\'\\"\\n            f\\":text=\'{safe_text}\'\\"\\n            f\\":fontsize={font_size}\\"\\n            f\\":fontcolor=white\\"\\n            f\\":borderw=2\\"\\n            f\\":bordercolor=black\\"\\n            f\\":x={x1}:y={y1}\\"\\n            f\\":enable=\'between(t,{t_start:.2f},{t_end:.2f})\'\\"\\n        )\\n        filters.append(drawtext)\\n\\n    return filters\\n\\n\\ndef _calc_font_size(text, bbox_w, bbox_h):\\n    \\"\\"\\"Calculate font size to fit translated text in the bbox.\\"\\"\\"\\n    text_len = len(text)\\n    if text_len == 0:\\n        return FONT_SIZE_MIN\\n\\n    char_width_ratio = 0.5\\n\\n    font_size_by_width = bbox_w / (text_len * char_width_ratio)\\n    font_size_by_height = bbox_h * 0.9\\n\\n    if font_size_by_width < FONT_SIZE_MIN:\\n        font_size_by_width_2line = bbox_w / (text_len * char_width_ratio / 2)\\n        font_size_by_height_2line = bbox_h * 0.45\\n        font_size = min(font_size_by_width_2line, font_size_by_height_2line, FONT_SIZE_MAX)\\n    else:\\n        font_size = min(font_size_by_width, font_size_by_height, FONT_SIZE_MAX)\\n\\n    font_size = max(int(font_size), FONT_SIZE_MIN)\\n    return font_size\\n\\n\\ndef _escape_ffmpeg_text(text):\\n    \\"\\"\\"Escape text for ffmpeg drawtext filter value.\\"\\"\\"\\n    text = text.replace(\\"\\\\\\\\\\", \\"\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\")\\n    text = text.replace(\\":\\", \\"\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\:\\")\\n    text = text.replace(\\"{\\", \\"\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\{\\")\\n    text = text.replace(\\"}\\", \\"\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\}\\")\\n    text = text.replace(\\"\'\\", \\"\\")\\n    return text\\n\\n\\n# ── Render with ffmpeg ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────\\ndef render_video(video_path, output_path, filters, video_info):\\n    \\"\\"\\"Render translated video using ffmpeg filter chain.\\"\\"\\"\\n    if not filters:\\n        logger.warning(\\"No filters to apply, copying video\\")\\n        subprocess.run([\\"cp\\", str(video_path), str(output_path)])\\n        return True\\n\\n    MAX_FILTERS = 100\\n\\n    if len(filters) <= MAX_FILTERS:\\n        return _render_single_pass(video_path, output_path, filters, video_info)\\n    else:\\n        drawbox_filters = [f for f in filters if f.startswith(\\"drawbox\\")]\\n        drawtext_filters = [f for f in filters if f.startswith(\\"drawtext\\")]\\n        logger.info(f\\"Multi-pass: {len(drawbox_filters)} drawbox + {len(drawtext_filters)} drawtext\\")\\n\\n        intermediate = output_path.with_suffix(\\".inpaint.mp4\\")\\n        if not _render_single_pass(video_path, intermediate, drawbox_filters, video_info):\\n            return False\\n\\n        result = _render_single_pass(intermediate, output_path, drawtext_filters, video_info)\\n        intermediate.unlink(missing_ok=True)\\n        return result\\n\\n\\ndef _render_single_pass(video_path, output_path, filters, video_info):\\n    \\"\\"\\"Single ffmpeg pass with given filters.\\"\\"\\"\\n    vf = \\",\\".join(filters)\\n    cmd = [\\n        \\"ffmpeg\\", \\"-y\\",\\n        \\"-i\\", str(video_path),\\n        \\"-vf\\", vf,\\n        \\"-c:v\\", \\"libx264\\",\\n        \\"-preset\\", \\"ultrafast\\",\\n        \\"-crf\\", \\"23\\",\\n        \\"-c:a\\", \\"copy\\",\\n        \\"-movflags\\", \\"+faststart\\",\\n        str(output_path)\\n    ]\\n\\n    logger.info(f\\"FFmpeg render: {len(filters)} filters\\")\\n\\n    try:\\n        result = subprocess.run(cmd, capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=1800)\\n        if result.returncode != 0:\\n            logger.error(f\\"FFmpeg failed: {result.stderr[-2000:]}\\")\\n            cmd_no_audio = [\\n                \\"ffmpeg\\", \\"-y\\",\\n                \\"-i\\", str(video_path),\\n                \\"-vf\\", vf,\\n                \\"-c:v\\", \\"libx264\\",\\n                \\"-preset\\", \\"ultrafast\\",\\n                \\"-crf\\", \\"23\\",\\n                \\"-an\\",\\n                \\"-movflags\\", \\"+faststart\\",\\n                str(output_path)\\n            ]\\n Direct match\\n    if text_clean in UI_LABEL_DICT:\\n        return UI_LABEL_DICT[text_clean]\\n    \\n    # 2. Text contains a known UI label as substring\\n    for jp, en in UI_LABEL_DICT.items():\\n        if jp in text_clean and len(text_clean) <= len(jp) + 6:\\n            return en\\n    \\n    # 3. Original was garbled OCR → translated to nonsense English\\n    - Translation contains unusual patterns\\n    - Very short katakana sequences that aren\'t real words\\n    \\"\\"\\"\\n    # If the original was properly matched by UI dict, it\'s not garbled\\n    if _is_ui_label(original) is not None:\\n        return False\\n    \\n    # If translation looks like nonsensical English (very short, unusual patterns)\\n    orig_stripped = original.strip()\\n    \\n    # Check for garbled katakana that got translated to nonsense\\n    katakana_only = re.sub(r\'[\\\\u30a1-\\\\u30ff\\\\uff66-\\\\uff9f\\\\u30fb\\\\u30fc\\\\u3000-\\\\u303f\\\\uff01-\\\\uff5e\\\\.。…、]\', \'\', orig_stripped)\\n    if len(katakana_only) == 0 and len(orig_stripped) <= 10:\\n        # All-katakana short sequence -
